   Ngokunjalo kangingekhohlwe ukubonga unkosikazi wami uNokuthula Ngubo (uMaHlatshwayo) obelokhu engigqugquzela ukuthi angiqede ukulibhala leli bhukwana, engitshela ukuthi ufisa kabi ukulibona selishicilelwe. Nalo-ke ngilinikezela kuyena kanye nasezinganeni zami, nakumama ongizalayo uMaDlamini. Kanti-ke nje, ngilethula ezandleni zabo bonke abantu abanothando lokufunda izincwadi ezilotshwe ngolimi lwakithi. Kodwa ngilinikezela ikakhulukazi entsheni, ngenjongo yokuchi kukhona okuncane ezokuhlomula kulamapheshana: Ningadinwa bakwerhu, kusasa siyodla okukhulu. Ngiyabonga.

unenkolelo ethi uma umuntu efunda izincwadi ezibhalwe ngeziliffii zendabuko zase-Aftika, nakanjani kufanele abe nolwazi oluthile ngamasiko nenkolelo, okuvamise ukuvezwa njengezinto ezingaguquki, okuyikho okuyizinsika zolwazinzulu nezindlela zokucabanga kwase-Aftika. 
   Lesisidingo sigcizelelwa kangangokuthi urn fundi walemibhalo uzizwa entula okuthile okungenakutholakala esikhathini azithola efunda ekuso, kwazise phela lamasiko nezinkolelo kuvamise ukukhonjwa Ie emuva, kusadliwa ngolud41a. Alikho iphutha empeleni ekugcizelelweni kosikompilo, inqobo nje lokhu kugcizelela kungaehumisi umqondo onhloso yawo kungukuthi abantu base-Aftika bamqondo munye ngokushiwo ngusikompilo lwesikhathi esithile. Empeleni ukubaluleka kokugeizelela usikompilo kubonakala lapho kunolunye, ikakhulukazi olufika nezifikanamthwalo, olusetshenziswa ngendlela enokuziqhayisa - indlela enikeza isithombe esingesona ngalolo abalufiee lapho behloma khona amadlangala. Kulesisimo, izifikanamthwalo zisebenzisa ukuhluka kosikompilo Iwazo njengesizathu esenza babe ngcono kunalaba abafikela kubo. Bayaye bangakuvezi ukuthi kuningi okungavunyelwana ngakho osikompilweni Iwalaba abafikela kubo, njengokuba osikompilweni lwabo kunokuningi ukushayisana kwemibono. Ake ngenze isibonelo esizothinta le-noveli kaMvukuzane, Amandl' Esambane, ukuze kubonakale ukuthi imibhalo yezifiki ngamasiko nenkambiso yase-Afrika isikhombisa okuningi ngokuziqhayisa kwabo, nokuqhakambisa ukuhluka kwabo kulabo ababathatha ngokuthi basesemuva, kunokuba isi tshele kabanzi ngalawomasiko nezinkambiso. 
   Kule-noveli uMvukuzane uxoxa udaba oluthinta isimo esithile esisatholakala ezindaweni ezithile esizweni samaZulu, lapho amantombazane ayekhethelwa ngoyise bawo abayeni, nakhu phela lokhu kwakusho ukwanda kwesibaya somukhwe. Kepha kuyaziwa ukuthi kulesisisimo kwakuvumelekile ukuba Iowa owayeseyithwalile intombazane ngale kwemvume yayo, ayemukwe yilowo eyayizikhethele yena. Phela isisho esithi 'oseyishayile akakayosi, oseyosile akakayidli noseyidlile usedle ieala', sisuselwa kuwo lomnqakiswano owawungapheliyo. Intombi yayisengabuyela kula eyayizikhombele yena, inqobo nje wayezimisele ukubuyisela izinkomo ezasezishaywe yilo wempoqo. Yize kukho konke lokhu intombazane isabonakala njengempahla yomashintshisana, kuyabonakala ukuthi inhloso kwakungekhona ukuyiphoqa ukuba igeine lapho ingakhombanga khona. hlangana kukaMqoqi noNobuhle ngasese, ukuze babonisane ngemizwa yabo ngodaba lokukhethelwa izithandwa zabo, kwenza kube lula ukwakha uzungu lokuchitha uzungu Iwabazali babo lokuba baganane ngale kwentando yabo. Ngalendlela ukufunda lendaba kuyasithuthukisa ngokomqondo, kanti kuphinde kugcizelele ukuthi noma ngabe yiliphi isikompilo linezindlela zalo zokulishintsha. 
   Ngigcizelela lend lela yokufunda lenovelingoba isenza sifunde ezinye izincwadi ezibhalwe ngezilimi zendabuko ngezindlela ezihlukile, izindlela ezenza kubonakale ukuthi imiphakathi iyizakhiwo ezingashintshwa. Izincwadi ezifana no Ngavele Ngasho ka David Mkhize noma u Mntanami! Mntanami! ka Sibusiso Nyembezi azikhulumi nje kuphela ngokungaziphathi kahle kwabalingiswa oDambuza no Jabulani, kepha okubaluleke kakhulu zikhuluma kabanzi ngenqubo yobandlululo nokufika kongxiwankulu, okwaletha imithetho. ethile yengcindezelo, nekuyiyona eyashintsha izindlela zokuphila kuleyomiphakathi eyayivele ishintsha ngezindlela eziningi. Lenoveli, Amandl' Esambane, ilandela wona lomkhakha, yize yona igcizelela ukushintsha kobudlelwane phakathi kwabesilisa nabes.ifaz~~e abakhulayo, emphakathini lapho ukushintsha kwawo kwakungafib ezlZlndeni lapho izinqumo ngempilo yabo zazithathwa khona. 
   Yingakho nje kungumbono wami ukuthi lenoveli ifanele ukufundwa yiningi elifuna ukuyihlamuka inkambiso eqhakambisa ukunga~uhlup~i umqondo, inkambiso egcizelela ubudlelwane obenza umphakathl ungazlbuzi ukuthi yiziphi izindlela ezintsha zokuhlaziya isimo okucacayo ukuthi sishintshile sobudlelwano phakathi kwamazinga ahlukene emphakathini: kwahesilisa nahesifazane, kwa:makhosi nahahuswayo, kwahafundile nabangafundile, kwabanothile nabampofu .. Ngaleyondlela kuyoba lula ukuqeda imfundisoze ethi izincwadi ezibhalwe ngezilimi zase-Aftika azisho lutho ngale kokuzingela, kwezimpi, njaJonjalo.

Isabluko Sokuqala 
Ernzini KaMbhekeni Zulu, K waDukuza 

"Yindoda!" Ayejwayele ukusho kanjalo amakhehla akwaDukuza uma ethamele isigcaki, egqolozele isithabathaba somuzi womfo kaMageba: 
   "Yindoda ngempela lomfana kaS'khonyane!" Ayesho aphindelele uma sekuntambama, lapho umhlambi wezinkomo zikaMbhekeni sewubonakala kahle, uklabe kulelo gcaki elingaphesheya komuzi. 
"Hha! Usho uMbhekeni! Phela yindoda yamadoda ngempela leyo!" 
Zazinanela zisho kanjalo izalukazi lapho sezithwele imithwadlwana yazo, zivela kokweleta esitolo sikaMbhekeni. 
â¢ 
â¢ 
â¢ 
â¢ 

Indawo yakwaDukuza edolobheni laseStanger, ingenye yezindawo ezidumile futhi ebalulekile emlandweni wesizwe samaZulu. Phela kulapho kukhona idlinza elifihle amathambo eLembe, inkosi ekuyiyona eyabumba isizwe samaZulu. Le ndawo-ke, yindawo ejwayelekile njengazo zonke ezikhona phansi komthunzi welanga. Abantu bakhile imizi yabo. Kukhona abantu bezibongo ezahlukahlukene, kukhona izigwili, abampofu, njalonjalo. Ngokunjalo-ke noMbhekeni Zulu, wayeyisakhamuzi esaziwayo kulendawo. Wayengagcinile nje ngokwaziwa kwaDukuza kuphela, kodwa wayedumile nje ezindaweni eziningi kuleli likaMthaniya. Phela umfo kaMageba 10 wayeyisigwili sangempela. Wayenesitolo eMpangeni kanti esinye siseShowe. Kanti lapha endaweni yakubo wayenamasimi omoba. Abantu ababewazi kahle umlando wakhe, babethi yiwona kanye lawo masimi awamlethela imali athenga ngayo izitolo lezo ayenazo. 
   Kulendawo yakubo-ke, wayakhe umuzi omkhulu, owawuwubona uzidlulela nje ukuthi hhayi, lona-ke umuzi womuntu osuthayo. Kanti wawugqame kahle kakhulu ngoba wawakhiwe endaweni eli thafa. Wawumuhle impela, wakhiwe ngendlela ephucukile yesimanje. Indlu yesakhiwo sabelungu yayakhiwe ngezitini ezibomvu, kodwa yapendwa yaba nombala of ana nse nesibhakabhaka. Phezulu yayifulelwe ngokhethe olubomvu, kukhona negalaji elalibukeka nalo Ii fuze umuzi lowo. Igceke lalilikhulu lihlanzekile, kanti umuzi wonke nje wawubiyelwe ngothango olumhlophe. lophaya ngezansi kude buduze nomuzi, kwakukhona izibaya ezintathu. Esinye 
... kwakungesezinkomo, esinye kungesamankonyane, kanti esinye kwakungesezimvu. Buqamama naso kwakukhona ihhoko lezinkukhu. Kuloinuzi-ke, wayeh!ala nenkosikazi yakhe uMaNsele ababembiza ngokuthi

okaLindamkhonto. Babenezingane ezimbili, uNobuhle kanye noSiyabonga. Lezizingane zabo zazifunda ekholeji laseManzimtoti, emishini eyaziwa ngokuthi kuse Adams. UNobuhle wayefunda ibanga leshumi kanti umfowabo uSiyabonga yena wayefunda elesishiyagalombili. 
   Nanamhlanje ngisalukhumbula kahle hie lolosuku mhlazane ngiphonsa amehlo emzini wakwaMageba. Kwakusemini bebade, ilanga likhiph'umkhov 'etsheni. UMbhekeni wayehleli ekameleni elikhulu elingaphambili, okwakuyikamelo lokuphumula. Wayezihlalele kusofa wakhe kanokusho, ephethe usiba lokubhala ngesandla, elokhu esayinda ezinye zezinewadi zamabhizinisi akhe. 
   Kwathi kusenjalo kwangena owakwakhe uMaNsele. Wangena ephethe ithileyi awafike walibeka phezu kwetafulana elineane elaliphambi komyeni wakhe. Wathi angalibeka kahle ngesizotha ithileyi lelo uMaNsele, wezwakala ekhuluma ngezwi elipholile ebhekise kumyeni wakhe wathi; "Uxolo baba, bengicela uke wehlise leli langa elishisa kangaka bandla ngalolu khanjana lwaleli bhodlela lesiphuzo esibandayo. Kade bandla Mageba uwuqalile lomsenzi wakho, kodwa kawukaze urhole lutho nje lokuqeda ukoma." Kusho uMaNsele ebambelele emadolweni ekhombisa inhlonipho, emoyizela ebuka umyeni wakhe. 
   "Ngiyabonga Lindamkhonto, yize khona nawe ubona ukuthi sewenze iphurha." Kusho uMageba engambhekile nokumbheka uMaNsele, elokhu eqhubeka nokusayinda amaphepha akhe. Athande ukumethusa lawo mazwi uMaNsele, asimze axakeke nje ukuthi ngabe iphutha lakhe likuphi. 
   Kodwa abuze ngesizorha kumyeni wakhe athi: "Hhawu baba, ngabe usho ukutliini uma urhi sengenze iphutha? Ngabe uehaza ukuthi sengikuphazamise kakhulu emsebenzini wakho? Ngesiphuzo nje baba.? Phela mina bengikulethele ngoba ngizwela wena kuleli langa elifuna ukusikhipha imiphefumulo." 
   Amoyizele uMageba athathe ibhodlela lelo likanemenayidi alivule, agewalise ingilazi maqedane athi uka isiphuzo leso bese eyibeka phansi. Aphenduke abuke uMaNsele bese emphendula ethi: "Hhayi nkosikazi, mina ka-. ngisho konke lokhu okueabangayo njengoba usho nje, kodwa ngihamba emazwini akho. Ngoba wena uthi kade ngiwuqalile lomsebenzi wami, kodwa kangikaze ngithole lutho nje lokuqeda ukoma. Ake usho-ke ukuthi sonke lesi sikhathi bewunganginiki ngani isiphuzo? Awuboni-ke ukurhi yiphutha lelo? Bengiehaza lokho-ke mina Lindamkhonto." Kusho uMageba ngokukhululeka. 
Wathi uma nje eqala ethi uyaphendula uMaNsele, kwangena uNobuhle. 
Wafika wakhothama ph.mbi kwabazali bakhe, wakhulumela phansi ngokuzithoba wathi; "Ngiyaxolisa bandla ngokungena nginiphazamise engxoxweni ebenisayixoxa. Impela kangihlosile ukuniphazamisa, kodwa bengithi angizobuza kubaba ukuthi ngingamnika yini na isiphuzo esibandayo, ukuze

athibe lelilanga elishisa kangaka. Kanti kangibuzanga elangeni, urnama usengeqelele ngaphambili." 
   Wathi ukuphakamisa ikhanda kaneane uyise, wabuye washesha wabheka amaphepha akhe, wakhuluma eqhubeka nokuwasayinda wathi; "Yebo ngempela kunjalo ndodakazi, useze wangieabangela unyoko. Eqinisweni-ke, kangazi ukurhi kuze kusukume yena nje, wena ulibele ukwenzani ngale ekameleni lakho. Kusho ukuthi ulibele ukulala! Hhi? Ulibele ukulala emini ka bha. He! Impela uma ngiqala ukubheka nje, sengathi usemningi umsebenzi okusafanele umuntu awenze lapha kuwena. Ngisho kusadliwa ngoludala impela, kayikaze nanini intombazane ilale emini. Uyazi mina Nobuhle bengithi kawukho laph 'ekhaya? Kanti ukhona, ulibele ukulala?" Abuze uMageba aze abuthe izinhlonze, aguqubale ngisho nasebusweni kubonakale ukuthi siyameasula impela lesi senzo sikaNobuhle. Abone noNobuhle ukuthi isimo sishubile, ajeqeze unina maqedane abheke phansi, asimze axakeke nje ukurhi uzophendula athini. Washeshe wabona noMaNsele ukurhi indodakazi yakhe isenkingeni, wazijuba waphendula wathi; "Hhawu baba, yiba sewumxolela bandla. Naye ngiyethemba ukuthi uzwile uBuhle. Futhi ngiyethemba kasobuye aphinde akwenze lokhu. Eqinisweni baba singathi ubesaphumule nje umntwana. Ngoba phela njengoba izikole zisavaliwe nje, vele bazophu ... " 
   Hha! Wasithinta isidleke sezinyosi uMaNsele, wangenela. ngolaka uMageba wathi; "MaNsele! Uyabona nje empilweni yami yonke jikelele, kayikho into engidina njengalena oyenzayo. Uyangizwa? Awubheke nje ngikhuluma nengane ngiyisola ngesenzo sayo esingesihle, wena sewuyayiphendulela, sewuyayixolisela sekunjeyaya! Okusho khona ukurhi bowuvele umbonile ukurhi ulele. Kwathi-ke ngoba nakhu uyamtotosa, wavele wamyeka nje! Hhi? MaNsele? Kodwa nenziwa yini ukuvuna izingane? Ngiyabuza phela phendula njengase kuqaleni. Habe! Wathula manje! Kusho ukurhi ukwazi ukuphendulela abanye abantu, uma sekuqondene nawe uyehluleka? Lalela-ke. ungaphinde uyenze lento."

Emzlnl KaMbhekeni Zulu. KwaDukuza 
   Kodwa phela eginisweni uMhhekeni wayethetha ngakhona, intomhazane kayilali emini. Kufanele ihonakale iyaluza yehla yenyuka phakathi kwekhaya, izijwayeze ukusehenza lize liyoshona. Ukuze nangesikhathi esizayo lapho isithole umendo ingahi yisehluleki uma iganele emzini omkhulu onahantu ahaningi ahangaphezu kwalapho izalwa khona. 
   Kodwa-ke uNohuhle yena wayengazange alale. Wayezihlalele nje phezu komhhede ekameleni lakhe, elokhu ehuka ihhuku elalinezithomhe zahangane hakhe ahekade efunda naho ekholeji laseManzimtoti. Wayehleli elihuka elokhu eliphenya kancane, umgondo wakhe ujulile nenhliziyo yakhe ihuhlungu. Phela njengalokhu sesizwile ukuthi kwase kungunyaka wakhe wokugcina lona eToti, yikho lokho kanye okwakumphethe kahuhlungu ngoha wayecahanga ngahangane hakhe ayesehlukene naho, futhi wayengazi noma hasayophinde hahonane yini na. 
   Ehhukwini lelo, kwakukhona izithomhe zamantomhazane kanye nezahafana ayehamhisana naho uma hedingida hehonisana ngezifundo zehanga labo ngesikhathi santamhama uma hehlangene ehholo lasekholeji. Kodwa amehlo akhe ayegxile kakhulu esithomheni somunye umfana ohekade engomunye wahahlakaniphe kakhulu ehangeni laho. lowo kwakunguSikhumhuzo Msomi, umfana wasenhla neNatali eMtshezi. 
   UNohuhle wezwa efikelwa umunyu uma ehuka lesi sithomhe somfo wakoNomndayi. Phela wayekhumhula indlela ehuhlungu akhula ngayo uKhumhi. Phela wayehatshele ukuthi uyambonga uSomandla ngoha ukwazile ukumthwala aze afinyelele kuleli banga leshumi, ngoha yena ufana nentandane. Uyise washona rena enezinyanga ezimbili nje vo ezelwe. Wakhuliswa uninalume, nokunguyena owayemfundisa sonke lesisikhathi. Ngakho-ke, ucela iNkosi ibe naye aphumelele, ukuze asebenze akwazi ukuhuyisa yonke lemali ahefundiswa ngayo uninalume. 
   Ngokunjalo fuchi emgondweni wakhe uNohuhle, waphinde wafikelwa yinkumhulo yesikhathi sakhe sokugcina ukuhonana noSikhumhuzo. Leso sikhathi phela kwakuntamhama ngosuku lwaho lokugcina eToti. Bahehleli bonke eHholo helinde isidlo sangokuhlwa. Izitshudeni zazincokola ngempilo ehezikade ziyiphila ngesikhathi zihlanganiswe yimfundo. kuleliKholeji. Zazijahule zifile zihonakala ukuthi ziyalithakasela leli thuha esezize zafinyelela kulo. Zazihonisana ngokuthi, lowo ahazali ahasenawo amandla , okumghuha aye phamhili nemfundo, kufanele ayemukele ngezandla nangenhliziyo emhlophe leyonselelo ngoha lelithuha liyivelakancane. Imfundo phela iyisikhali esingasoze saphuka nanini, kanti-ke iyilona zihuko eliyosiwelisela ngaphesheya emadlelweni aluhlaza. Kanti ngokunjalo nalaho ahazali haho asehephelelwe ngamandla njengamanje, akufanele hangenwe ngamanzi emadolweni. Kodwa kufanele hawe hevuka, hazame ngezindlela zonke ukughuhekela phamhili. Vele kakade umuntu ufunda aze afe. . 
 
Amandl' Esambane 
   Zaxoxa kahanzi impela izitshudeni ngaleyontamhama. Zanikezana amakheli asemakhaya azo kanye nezithomhe. Yilezo zithomhe-ke ezazihukwa uNohuhle ekameleni lakhe. Kanti Nohuhle ndini wawuhuka isithombe sika Sikhumbuzo nje, It. enhla eMtshezi, ngaso belu isikhathi esifanayo, noSikhumbuzo wayehleli ekameleni lakhe kanye nomunye umngani wakhe. Babezihlalele bexoxa, esandleni sakhe ephethe isithombe sentombi yakwaMageba, intokazi yakwaDukuza eStanger. Wayexoxela umngani wakhe ngobuhle kanye nenhlonipho yalentokazi. Impela wayefunga egomela okaNomndayi ethi, yize engumfokazane, kodwa uzoyibhalela intokazi kaMageba ayibonise ukuchi ufisa babambisane kwezothando ukuze bakhe umuzi wabo ogotho wakusasa. 
   Wathi angaligeda ukulibuka ibhuku lelo lezithombe uNobuble, walivala waliphindisela lapho wayelithathe khona. Wagala wabuya umgondo, wakhumbula imisebenzi okwakufunele ayenze yasekhaya. Wacabanga ukuthi kufanele agale ngokwenzela uyise isiphuzo sokuqeda ukoma. Nakho-ke ethi thwasu egonda ekameleni lokuphumula lapho uyise wayehleli khona, kanti uzofika ahlangane nembibizane. 
   Kodwa baxolisa kanye kanye nonina uMaNsele ngamaphutha abo kuMageba, baphuma belandelana bamshiya yedwa. 
   Wasala waghubeka nokusayinda izincwadi zakhe uMbhekeni waze waziqeda. Wathi angageda, wakhumbula ukuthi kufanele abhalele umfowabo ozalwa nguyis'omncane owayakhe kwaMagoda esifundeni saseRichmond .. Phela wayemazise ngomsebenzi omkhulu awayezowenza khona lapha emzini wakhe kwelakubo kwaDukuza. Kulomsebenzi, kwabe kuzohlatshwa izinkomo kudliwe kubuswe kube njeyaya. Phela uMageba wayezobe enza umemulo wendodakazi yakhe eyabe iligugu elikhulu kuyena. Lowo-ke kwakuyinkosazane yekhaya, uNobuhle. Umsebenzi lowo womemulo, wawuzokuba ngayo kanye inyanga kaZibandlela.

kubanga izins~ku ezingaki, yafika inewacli leyo kwaMagoda eRichmond. Umfowabo kaMbhekeni wajabula kakhulu ukuzwa izindaba ezimnandi kangako. Lowo phela kwakuyindodana kayis'omneane, igama layo kunguZwelonke. 
UZwelonke lona-ke, wayeyisakhamuzi esaziwayo esigodini sakwaMagoda. 
Okwakumenza abe nedumela ukuthi ngesikhathi esasebenza, wayekade esebenza ngaphansi kombutho wamaphoyisa kahulumeni, esebenza njengomseshi. Wayaziwa ngekhono ayekade enalo ngesikhathi esangufokisi. Kodwa wayesathatha umhlalaphansi. Yize kodwa wayesedla endala umfo kaMageba, uma nje eke wakubhadama uganga, wayengalilindi ibhadi. Wayesimze ayimise ngokushesha imoto yakhe, ngokuphazima kweso, adonse izulu lezandla akukhombe ngalo, akugalele amasongo kaSigonyela, akuhlohloloze akufake emotweni yakhe. Hhawu uwena lowo kanye naye nilibangisa esiteshini samaphoyisa esiseduze nalapho ekubambele kho.na, uye kolala endlini emnyama njalo. Okusho ukuthi nje, izifungo awayezenze mhla ejoyina emaphoyiseni wayesazikhumbula njengoba zazinjalo. Futhi-ke wayeqhubeka nazo ngokukhulu ukwethembeka. Ngakho-ke igama lakhe lalilokhu ligqame njalo embuthweni wamaphoyisa nasemphakathini. 
   Wayenomuzi kanokusho naye lapha kwaMagoda. Abantu babe mhlonipha kakhulu futhi elithemba emphakathini wakubo. Bheka ngoba kwakuthi uma kunenkulumo eshubile komkhulu, ayixazulule ngobuhlakani obukhulu leyonkinga umfo kaMageba. Wayeyieaeisa kahle ngobuciko inkulumo, akhulume kuse geqe emadodeni, kueaeelwe ngisho nesigxaza amathe. Urn the tho wayewazi njengoba azi ingemuva lesandla sakhe. 
   Yilokho-ke nokwamenza waba ngumngane omkhulu wenkosi. Kanti-ke nje, abantu babemkhulekela uZwelonke bembiza ngoNdabezitha wangoqobo, bembiza ngoMntwana. Phela bonke abantu bakwaZulu ngesibongo bayakhulekelwa, babizwa ngoNdabezitha ngoba yibona abangamakhosi ohlanga kwelikaMthaniya. Njengoba-ke sesizwile ukuthi wayengumngane omkhulu wenkosi, ngempela Ialingapheli isonto bengavakashelananga. 
   Namhlanje sihlangana naye urn fa kaMageba kungolweSine, ngezikhathi zehora leshumi ekuseni. UMntwana uhleli nomndeni wakhe. Phela njengoba kuyinyanga kaZibandlela nje, amadodana lawa abuyile eNdaleni lapho efunda khona. lIanga lalikhipha inhlanzi emanzini. Abafana babezihlalele nje elawini labo, bezineokolela izindarshana zabo ezingasho lutho.

             Isahluko Sesithathu Komkhulu, Enkosini USihlangusempi 
l
nkosi yasendaweni yakwaMagoda, uSihlangusempi Dlamini, kwakungesiyena umuntu ozulayo. Wayehamba nje uma eyolungisa izinto ezithile zesizwe sakhe enkantolo. Yize wayengumuntu onamabhizinisi ezimota ezazithutha abantu abasuka edolobheni eRiehmond, beya eMgungundiovu, kodwa wawungeke urn bone elokhu egealuza phakathi kwazo. Kanti futhi uyena owakomkhulu owayenamabhasi amabili awayehamba phakathi kwendawo yakwaMagoda nasedolobheni. 
   UNdabezitha lona, inkosi yesizwe saseNhlangwini, wayengakabi mdala kangako. Kodwa ngenxa yempilo yakhe eyase ibuthaka, wayesefuna ukusishiya isikhundla sakhe sobukhosi. Kodwa phela wayefuna ukusishiyela indodana yakhe uMqoqi. UMqoqi lona-ke, wayefunda esikoleni samakhosi kwaNongoma, esibizwa ngokuthi kuseBhekuzulu. Njengoba-ke sesizwile ukuthi lena kwakuyinyanga kaZibandlela, ngokunjalo-ke noMqoqi wayebuyile eSikoleni. Futhi wabe eseziphothulile izifundo zakhe zobukhosi. 
   Namhlanjena-ke njengoba kungoLwesine nje, uMqoqi wayevuke ekuseni wathatha imota yakhe, wahamba nomngane wakhe uthisha uMzolo bathi basalibhekisa edolobheni, laseMgungundlovu. Ukuthi-ke babeyokwenzani lapho, hhayi-ke, akudokwe eligayelwa thina lelo. Kodwa ngineqiniso lokuthi koZohamba kuhambe, size sizwe ukuthi yini lena ababeyihambele kulelidolobhakazi. Phela akukho okufihlakala unomphelo lapha kwamhlaba. 
   Ngesikhathi uZwelonke efika komkhulu, inkosi yayikhona izihlaleie kuvulandi wendlu yayo kanokusho. Yayizihlalele nje ibuka amasimu ayebonakala emable elinyiwe. Kanri iaphaya ezansi, yayiwubuka nomfula ugeleza, lapha emaeeleni osebeni lwawo wawuhlotshiswe izihlahla zemvelo. Ezomnyezane zaziyikazela zisho ngamaqabunga aluhlaza ewe. Kanti eziny'izinhlobonhlobo, zaziqhakaze izimbali ezinhle ezimibalabala. Kwakuthaphuka amakha ammnandi emvelo, izinyosi ziwele ngelibanzi. 
   Njengoba inkosi yayihleli kuvulandi nje, kuningi eyayikubuka. Bheka ngoba yayiwabona namadoda asesigodini sayo e1}lezi phansi komthunzi ngase sibayeni komunye umuzi wakwaNdlovu, owawungaphesheya komfula obhekene nakomkhulu. Ayehleli phansi, kudamane kubonakala kulokhu kusukuma ngayinye ithi ukuhamba ibangana nje ilishiya igeeke lakwaNdlovu, bese iguqa ngedolo elilodwa iehi the amanzi, ibuye iphindele kwamanye phansi komthunzi. Impela kwakubonakala ukuthi zinoju kwaGatsheni. Ngiyethemb!, ukuthi amaningi alala engembethe.

Komkhulu. Enkoslnl USlhlangusempl 

phela zazizitika ngezithelo zamapetshisi, kanti yena owakomkhulu wayeheke ihhikili lamahewu phamhi kwakhe, awayedamane ethi ngqa kulona ecima ukoma. Phela amponjwana wayengawathi mhihi nangengozi. Lilonke-ke nje; izwe lalilihle kubonakala ukuthi ihlobo lifike qathatha nezinqotho zalo. 
   Hhayi-ke, kwathi kusenjalo kwezwakala imoto iduma egcekeni.Yafika yema waphuma lowo owayeyishayela. Wathi eqamhe ephuma, yahe inkosi seyimoyizela, ngoha yase ihonile ukuthi imoto leyo ngekahani. Kanti ngokunjalo noMntwana uZwelonke waphuma emamatheka, ejahuliswa ukuthi umfice ekhona ekhaya owakomkhulu, futhi wamfica kahle ezihlalele yedwa. 
   Wafika wema kude huduze nenkosi, isigqoko esesiphethe ngesandla, maqedane wakhuleka njengenjwayelo. kuyona bafike bakhuleke. Hhayi-ke, ivele igane esokeni kumfo kaGatsheni ngoba naye wayevele akhiphele isandla ngaphandle kuqala, avume ngomusa aze anqekuzise kaningi ikhanda. Abantu-ke bavele bakholwe ukuthi iyona uqobo inkosi lena. 
   Emva kwesikhashana sebethe nje ukuphuma kancane edolobheni, sebeqala ukungena umgwaqo omkhulu olibangise koMgungundlovu, baphuma ezimotweni bavalelisa. Babuyela emuva ababuyayo, baqhubekela phambili ababelibangise eStanger kwaDukuza. 
   Endleleni eqonde kwaDukuza, inkosi kanye noMageba babezincokolela nje bekhululekile. Kanti uZondi yena wayengakhulumi lutho, kuphela nje ephendula lokho okubuzwayo, abuye athule agqolozele umgwaqo. Wawungathi uyaqala ukushayela, kanti lutho. Yikho nje. ukuthi inhliziyo yakhe yase ile kwaDukuza lapho ayengakaze alubhade nakanye. 
Barhi uma befika edolobheni IaseThekwini, bathi ukuma isikhashana. 
Phela uZwelonke wayefuna ukushayela umfowabo uMbhekeni ucingo, emazisa ukuthi usefike qathatha nenkosi yaseNhlangwini. Kodwa wenza iphutha angazange ali bone yena ukuthi uyalenza ngaleso sikhathi. Phela kazange ambale uZondi owayezimisele ngokuthi uzofika abizwe ngenduna yaseNhlangwini. 
   Akubanga isikhathi esingakanani, hhiya, batheleka kwaDukuza. Kazi uZondi ayezofezeka yini amaphupho akhe awayewahlebele amadoda ngesikhathi esho amazwi athi: "Ngicela ungizwe kahle wakithi. Njengoba ngithi abantu bakwaDukuza bazobe bengibiza ngenduna nje, angisho ukuthi bazobe betshelwe yimina noma inkosi noma uMtwana uZwelonke. Qha, akunjalo wakithi. Kodwa kuzobe kuzisholo bona nje abantu bakhona, besho bengasibuzanga. Bazobe beshiso indlela engizobe ngiyiyona." 
   Kazi ndlelani lena awayeyiyona okaNondaba ngalolusuku? Ngoba wayengaqali nje ukuswenka agqoke isudi! Noma wayecabanga ukuthi abanru baKwaZulu kuseyilabaya bamabheshu? Amasudi lutho nje, kawaziwa? Impela asazi. Kodwa esikwaziyo ukuthi base betheleke ngezinkani kwaDukuza, futhi sebephakathi emagcekeni omuzi kaMbhekeni.

Umemulo kaNobuhle. Indodakazl KaMbhckenl 

Futhi ngineqlnlso lokuthi, noma iNkosi yayimuphe ingane eyisidalwa esinhloboni, wayevele ngalolusuku eyosihlanganisa kanjena uMageba ukuze simbongele kuSomandla ngesithombe amuphe sona, ngoba uNkulunkulu akasolwa. Yebo khona njengoba silapha nje, izinhliziyo zethu kazifani. Kukhona abeze ngobubi, ngoba nje bephethwe yisifo somona. Kodwa-ke noma kunjalo muzi wakwaMageba, kufanele konke lokho sikwamukele. Ngoba kuyingxenye yezilingo zalomhlaba. Ngisho ngithi-ke, noma kungavelani lapha phakathi kwalomuzi uma lomsebenzi usudlulile, kodwa nize nibambelele kulamazwi angewele athi: "Mbonge uJehova mphefumulo wami, nakho konke okuphakathi kwami, akubonge igama likaJehova." 
   Abantu babethule belalele ngesizotha. Kuphela nje kwakuzwakala ukukhwehlela, kodwa bezama ukuzibamba. Inkonzo leyo yavalwa ngomthandazo owenziwa ngomunye womame, naye owahamba khona emazwini okubonga. Kwenziwa isibusiso yaphuma inkonzo. Banke abantu babengayivali imilomo, bencoma intshumayelo kaMfundisi uBhengu. 
   Hhiya, kwaqhutshekelwa phambili nohlelo lombuso. Kwakhala imishini yokudansa, kwazise phela kwakukhanya bha njengasemini ngoba ugesi wawujikeleze umuzi wanke. Hhayi-ke, yagan'esokeni entsheni yempueuko, izitika ngomdanso. Wababona abanye berne ngezithende belokhu beshaya kaneane phansi ngezinzwane benyakazisa amahlombe, beqalaza ngapha nangapha, beshaya izithupha emoyeni. Kwabonakala impela ukuthi lukhulu abalwenzayo. 
   Kanti ngokunjalo ngapha ngasohlangothini lwezintokazi, nakhona kwaku ehiz'ukotsh'efusini. Bheka ngoba zabonakala nazo sezigobe kaneane zikheee izisu. Amadolo seziwaghuhe phamhili, zilnkhu ziwanyakazisa kaneane ngokushiyana zimi mazonzwane. Izandla lezi wena? Wo! Ngiyakutshela! Esinye sibambelele esiswini, kanti esinye silokhu sishaya izithupha emoyeni. Impela kudela owayelapho. Injabulo yayibhalwe ebusweni kuye wonke umuntu. Wawungafunga ugomele uthi usizi kabakaze babe nalo ilokhu bazalwa. 
   Zahamba izikhathi, kwabonakala ukuthi abantu kufanele babuye bayophumula bangaphiki nentsha. Ngokunjalo-ke nezivakashi eziphambili zaseRiehmond zalungiselwa indawo yokulala efanele zona, zahamba zaya khona. Ngempela zazibheme zakholwa ubuhle nobukhulu bombuso ezazihlangabezana nawo kwaMbhekeni. Impela babezofika bayixoxe beyixoxile indaba emuva ekhaya Ie kwaMagoda eNhlangwini. 
   Abantu abanhlobonhlobo babebulala inyoka lapha emzini wakwaMageba. Bheka ngoba kwakukhona izingane ezineane, kuye kofika kulabo abamnkantsh'ubomvu, ongubo seziya eweni. Okwakubonakala ukuthi kade babedliwa oKhisimusi yilaba bantu bol Kukhona izimpunyela ezidla izambane likapondo kanye nezimpofana ezishaya inja ngekhanda. Kwaku-

   Kanti bandla lurho nje, ikhehla lalingazange liyithi vu indaba yentombi yakwaDukuza. Futhi lalingazange layitshela muntu naleyo yentombi yaseMgungundlovu. Ngisho uMqoqi imbala, lalingazange limtshele ukuthi ialike lambona ereremuka eMgungundlovu. Lahlebela inkosi nje lageina. 
Inkosi yabuye yangena endlini yahlala phansi, yaphendula uMqoqi yathi: 
"Cha ndodana, bengingazi ukuthi kanti uma uhleli laph'ekhaya uyaziqaphela izinto ezenzekayo. Impela njengoba ubuza nje, nami angazi ukurhi lamadoda azohamba kanjani. Mhlawumbi nje azohamba ekamabuya ze lapho ngiwathume khona".

   Hhayi-ke, indaba yembizo yasakazeka ngokushesha kuyo yonke indawo yaseNhlangwini. Uthisha uMzolo yena kwakuthi akazibulale ngenxa yenjabulo. Phela wayesebona ukuthi uhambo Iwakhe IwaseMgungundlovu sekufike esikhathini sokuthi izithelo zalo zivunwe.

   Waphendula ngokukhulu ukunganaki uMaNguse wathi: "000, phela baba ngathi, siyoyieela ivuthiwe. Kodwa sengaze ngabona ukuthi ngeke size sieele lutho ngoba kakuphekwe lutho kuloluhambo Iwenu. Ngakho-ke, ngeke kuze kuvuthwe lutho."

   UMgogi wayeselulangazelele kabi usuku lwembizo. Kodwa lendaba yalembizo wayigeina esifubeni sakhe wangamazisa uNombuso.    Angithi phela uthisha uMzolo ngenxa yenjabulo, wahamba udaba lwembizo wayolwazisa amahhovisi ashieilela izindaba zaleli phephandaba khona eMgungundloVu. Phela wayenzela ukuthi bonke abantu baseNhlangwini, ngisho abasebenza emadolobheni, balwazi loludaba.

athi ingachitheka imbizo, abonakala amadoda engena emizini eseduze nakomkhulu. Phela kwase kuyisikhathi sokwehlisa lelolanga elalishisa kuhle komlilo. Nekhehla lakwaMrhembu lalimdibi munye namadoda lawo. Layidonsa ngamatomu injomane yalo, lizincokolela nalawo elalihamba nawo. Bahamba bayongena komunye umuzi wakwaMncwabe, inkuxa nje yakwabo yendoda. Kanti laphaya emuva komkhulu, uZwelonke kanye nalabo awayakade ehleli nabo ngaphambili embizweni, basala baxoxela inkosi ngakho konke okwenzekile, nanokuthi izingxoxo zembizo leyo zigcinephi 
   UZwelonke wayethukuthele efa ukufa lokhu. Wayichazela konke inkosi, wawasho wawaphindelela amazwi kaMzolo. Wathi umhlambalaze wamqeda phambi kwesizwe saseNhlangwini. Kusale khona nje ukuthi angamkhotnbi ngomunwe emehlweni. Futhi nawo amadoda avele azithulela nje. Okusho khona ukuthi nawo anelisekile yindelelo ekhulunywe uMzolo. "Impela abantu laba kabathembekile neze." Washo egcizelela. 
   Ngaso souke leso sikhathi, iukosi yayi thule ilalele ngesizotha. Kanti emqondweni wayo yayilokhu ithatha ibeka. Ekugcineni yezwakala ikhulumela phansi kodwa isho ngesigqi yathi: "Yebo-ke bakwethu, sengikuzwe konke okwenzekile embizweni. Futhi ngiyabona ukuthi nendodana irharhekile impela yileyo ntombi yaseMbo. Yize khona irhe isazoqala ibone intombi yakwaMageba. Kodwa lokho kakunginiki irhemba lokurhi iyowuguqula umqondo wayo uma isiyibonile. Ngakho-ke, kuzofanele sisheshe siyihambele phambili. Ukuze irhi iqambe izame ukwenza okunye, sibe sesiyibambe ngobhongwane. Angikwazi mina ukurhi ngingalahlekelwa ubulingane bakwaMageba. Impela ngiyokwehluleka ngizamile. Kade mina ngangibona. Ningesabi lutho." Yasho yarhi ukumoyizela. 
   Amadoda lawo alalela ngenkulu inhlonipho ngesikharhi ikhuluma inkosi. Yawachazela-ke ngesu eseyilibophile, ukuze uMqoqi angakwazi nakancane ukuyikhahlela intombi kaMbhekeni. Yawarshela ukuthi izokwenza indumezulu yedili ilenzele uMqoqi. Yarhi izomrshela kwezikabhoqo ukurhi idili lelo imenzela ngoba ekhombisa ukuyihlonipha yona kanye nesizwe kukho konke. Futhi ngendlela eyakhuluma ngayo inkosi, wonke amadoda abonakala ekhululekile. Kwakhanya impela ukurhi hhayi; iyobe ilukhuni inkosana uma irhathe enye indlela. 
   Kanti inkosi yayixoxa nezinduna zayo nje, ngokunjalo namadoda ayexoxa ngalo udaba Iwembizo lapho ayekhona. Yebo-ke khona asingeke siyibale yonke imizi ekwangenwa kuyona, kodwa nje sesingabalula wona nje 10 wakwaMncwabe, lapho iningi lamadoda laphuma embizweni layongenisa

agingqika zalandelana izinsuku, Iwaze lwafika nosuku 1010 lwedili. KwakunguMgqibelo futhi, ekupheleni kwenyanga kaNdasa njengalokhu kwakumenyezelwe. Izulu lalilihle impela, lithe gqwa gqwa ngamafu esibhakabhekeni, wena owabona amabal'engwe, noma-ke izikhala zemithi. Lalibukeka sengathi nalo liyaluhlonipha futhi liyaluthakasela lolusuku lokuncoma inhlonipho yenkosana yaseNhlangwini. 
Uma uyibuka imizi yaseNhlangwini, yayimihle ngokunye kulezonsuku. 
Phela yase icakwe yabamhlophe, eminye iluhlaza, kuya ngokuthi imibala yayo ivuselelwe nje, beyikade injani ekuqaleni. Amagceke-ke wona, angisayiphathi indaba yawo. Ayeshanelwe ahlanzeka aba obani! Impela kwakubonakala ukuthi lukhulu luzokwenzeka namhlanje. Izinkomo zazizohlatshwa ngawo uMgqibelo lowo, bese kuyadliwa futhi ngalo kanye 1010suku. Kanti imizi leyo yayilungiswe kahle kangako nje, yayilungiselelwe isivakashi esasizofika njengesimenywa esiqavile edilini lelo. Futhi-ke, sasilindelwe ngamehlo abomvu abantu baseNhlangwini. Ingabe kwaku ngubani lesosivakashi? Habel kwakungabuye kube ubani! Phela kwakuyisimenywa esasivela kwaDukuza. Igama laso kunguMbhekeni Zulu, isiqumama esasesithathwa njengomlingane wakusasa wenkosi uSihlangusempi. 
   K wabonakala ekuseni ngalowoMgqibelo abantu baseNhlangwini bethe chithi saka begcwele izindlela zonke, amabombo bewabhekise komkhulu. Njengenhlalayenza, amadoda ayehamba ngezinyawo nanga mahhashi kanye nezimoto. Kanti omame nezintombi, nabo babonakala beshaye ujenge ezindleleni beqonde khona komkhulu. 
   Babethwele izimbiza zigcwele utshwala namahewu, abanye bethwele izinkwa ezibhakiwe, belethe izipheko komkhulu. Izinsizwa zazivunule zico- 
* nsa, zisho ngamabheshu namahawu azo amibalabala. Kanti abafanyana abazalwa yizinduna, bona babonakala beqhuba izimbuzi ngambili bebheke khana komkhulu. Angithi phela izinduna zazivumelane ngo~uphekisa inkos; ngezimbuzi ezimbili iyinye. Kanti nabanumzane abasuthayo babengazibekiIe phansi. Nabo baphonsa esivivaneni ngalokho ababefisa ngakha, imbuzi noma imvu. Izinkukhu-ke zona, zazimdibi munye emithwalweni yabanye omame. 
   Inkosi kayizange ichithe sikhathi, yathi akuhlatshwe izinkabi zayo ezinhlanu ezazise sibayeni, okuyizona eyayenzela ngazo inkosana idili. Ikhomba ezinjani zona ukukhuluphala wena bo! '-,' 

sekile ngaphakathi ngoba umuntu 10 ukhuluma ngesizotha, kanti ngisho nalapho umbheka, uyabona nje ukuthi chI', lena insizwa ziphelele ngempela. Lona-ke igama lakhe uSikhumbuzo Msomi, insizwa yasenhla neNatali Ie, eMtshezi. 

   Angazi-ke noma Ie mambane usayikhumbula yini na! Phela ilowaya Sikhumbuzo Msomi, uKhumbi, umfo wakoNomdayi owayefunda noNobuhle eKholeji laseManzimtoti emishini yase'Adams'. Lowaya Khumbi owayethathe ingqondo kaNobuhle mzukwane ebuka ibhuku lezithombe zabangane bakhe abekade efunda nabo eToti. Kanti wayilibuka nje, nakhona Ie eMtshezi, uSikhumbuzo nomngane wakhe babegqolozele isithombe sikaNobuhle. Sizokhumbula ukuthi umfo wako Nomndayi waze wafunga wagomela wathi, yize engumfokazane, kodwa uzozama ngezindlela zonke ukuyibhalela intokazi yakwaMageba, ayibonise ngokuthi ufisa babambisane kwezothando. Ukuze bakhe umuzi wabo oqotho wakusasa. 

   Ngempela-ke wakwenza lokho umfo kaMsomi. Wawa phezu kwamaphepha, wayichazela lonke iqiniso ngesifiso sengaphakathi lakhe. Pho, 11'chaza lageqa amagula iciko lakwabo. UNobuhle wafikelwa omkhulu umunyu ngalentandane ayeyazi ubunjalo bayo. Wazibuza waziphendula. Kodwa isithombe sosizi 10mtakaMsomi, salokhu simile emehlweni engqondo. Inhliziyo yakhe yehla yenyuka kuyena ngaphakathi ifuna indawo yokuphumula kodwa yangayithola. Wabona kungcono ayikhululele ingane yasemaSomini. Nangempela 'yawuthola umthunzi onentokozo. Nakho-ke sebephinda bezosebenza ndawonye edolobheni laseThekwini. 

   UNobuhle usematheni kangaka nje Ie eNhlangwini eRichmond, yena akazi nanyaka. Futhi akazange nje ezwe lutho oluphathelene nalolo dabI'. Yebo khona wezwa ukuthi uyise uzovakashela Ie eNhlangwini, kodwa konke lokho wangakufaki nakancane nje emqondweni wakhe. Bheka ngoba akuzange kumfikele ngisho nokuthi atshele uyise amkhonzele enkosini uSihlangusempi. Yize esandleni sakhe wayefake lona lelowashi ayelithengelwe yiyona. Angithi phela uKhumbi wayemphambanise ingqondo. Uthando lwabo Iwaluvutha amalangabi. 
Kulamahhovisi oMshuwalense-ke, uMbhekeni ujwayele ukufika kuwona. 

Usuke ezozilungisela izinto zakhe eziqondene noMshuwalense lowo, njengoba phela ujoyine wonI'. Kukaningana urnI' kwenzeke waqondana nokufika kusemini ngezikhathi zamadina, amfice uNobuhle ezihlalele ngenkulu intokozo nenye insizwa amtshela ukuthi isebenza ePosini. Wathi bajwayelene nje, ngoba nakhu babefunda kanye kanye eManzimtoti. 

   UMbhekeni waqala wangayithwaleli amehlo lendaba. Kodwa kwathi lapho eseyibona njalo lenhlangano yalezizingane, waqala wasola ukuthi kukhona okushaya amanzi. Waze wazijuba ngolunye usuku, wazama ukuphenyI' uNobuhle ngalomngane wakhe. Kodwa no Nobuhle akazange alokhu

Kucushwa Izlntambo Zolwembu 
   Walalela ngesineke uNobuhle. Waqala walukhumbula usuku Iwamadoda amahlanu aseNhlangwini evakashele kubo. Wethuka lapho esezwa ukuthi, sekuze kwabakhona nembizo eNhlangwini kuxoxwa ngaye? Yena engazi lutho? Hha! Esebona nje! Alahle uKhumbi wakhe? Impela kungavele kuchitheke gula linamasi. NoMqoqi wamtshela ukuthi yena uthandana nentombi yaseMbo. Wayixoxa nendaba kathisha uMzolo osebizwa ngo'Makadebona.' Yayilokhu ilalele njalo ngesizotha intombi yakwaMageba. Kodwa yathi ukumamatheka uma uMqoqi ephatha igama lika'Makadebona.' Yashesha yalithola isu okufanele balisebenzise benoMqoqi, ukuze kusheshe kuhlukane inhloko nesixhanti. Yamchazela ngesu lelo, naye uMqoqi wazizwa egculisekile. 
   Kazi lalithini! Kodwa phela akukho okufihlakala unomphelo lapha emhlabeni. Futhi-ke lona isu lelo, phela lalizovela obala ngoba vele babezolisebenzisa. UNobuhle waze waphetha ngamazwi athi, kuhle babambelele othandweni Iweqiniso. Yasho yaphindelela intokazi kaMageba ukuthi izimisele nakanjani ukusithwala isiphambano sothando Iwayo noKhumbi, ukuze ekugcineni izuze umvuzo wokuhlala kahle ngoxolo nenjabulo. 
"Kufanele sizicabangele ukuze sithole umvuzo wokuhlala ngentokozo. 
Ngisho neNkosi uJesu wavuma ukusithwala isiphambano ayezobethelelwa kusona, ngoba wayewazi umvuzo walokho. Namhlanje kuthiwa uyena oyindlalifa yasezulwini, lapho ehleli khona ngasekunene sikayise." Wagcizelela kanjalo-ke uNobuhle. 
   Babuyela ehhotela bethokozile ngesu elalizobakhulula kulawo maketango ababeboshelelwe ngawo. Kwase kuyibo abase becuphe izintambo zolwembu. Kwathi ntambama uma seligamenxe ihota lesihlanu, hhiya lachitheka idili. Kwangenwa ezimorweni, kwayilabo babamba ebebeze ngayo.

bekhotha imilomo. Yayimhlophe bheka! Ungafunga uthi bonke bebekade bedla ubhontshisi. Ngingabala ngithini bandlal Ngingathi nfe, izwe laliyixwayile imvelo. 
   Kanti kwabanye abantu baseNhlangwini, sengathi kwakubika ukudumala okukhulu okwakuza kukhankasile ngalowoMgqibelo. Asazi-ke ukuchi kwakubabele bani. Njengenhlala yenza-ke phela, amadoda abonakala ethe nzi izitshalagwayi, egcwele izinkalo namathafa elibhekise khona komkhulu. Yebo . khona ayehamba encokola kodwa hhayi njengasemihleni. Phela amakhaza akamngane kabani. 
   Ayefika akhuleke njengenjwayelo, maqedane ablale enkundleni. Nekhehla lakwaMthembu kanye nothisha uMzolo babekhona. Baxhawulana bobabili babuzana impilo. Ikhehla lake lasibamba isikhathi eside isandla sikaMzolo, lilokhu limthe njo ezinhlamvini zamehlo. Lambuka ngamehlo agcwele usizi, kwabonakala ukuthi liyamzwela ngenhliziyo. Naye uMzolo washesha wawufunda lowombhalo owawulotshwe emehlweni ekhehla. Kodwa wavele wamoyizela kancane wezwakala ethi: "Hhayi bab'uMvelase, ungesabi lucho: Phela asikezwa ukuthi icala lizolahla bani. Ungakhohlwa ukuthi kusemhlabeni lapha. Ngakho-ke, kusakusa." 
   Wathi angasho kanjalo uchisha uMzolo, avele ayeka ngisho izindaba ayezixoxa amadoda awaseduze kwakhe. Aphenduka ambheka ngokumangala. Waphinda waqhubeka okaMzolo wathi: "P.hela baba, kuyenzeka ngesinye isikhathi lithathe ongezansi limbeke ngasenhla, kuthi ongasenhla limkhiphele emnyango." 
Hhayi-ke wathi angasho kanjalo, ezwakala evungazela amadoda. 
Kwabonakala ukuchi athi hhiya, useyaziqinisa nje. Naye uMzolo wakubona lokho. Kodwa waphinde wamoyizela wazikhulumela nekhehla wathi: "Ngempela baba ngiqinisile. Abangaziyo ukuthi ngihlala ngikhuluma amaqiniso, sebeze bangibiza ngokuchi hhayi, lomfana kaMzolo, uMakadebona'. Ngiyakutshela baba." 
   Wathi angasho kanjalo, ngquzu insini emadodeni. Avele abona ukuthi kanti uyazintelela nje, uzama ukubatshela ukuchi leligama asebizwa ngalo useyalazi. Kwathi kusenjalo, yaphuma inkosi endlini nezinduna zayo kanye noMqoqi. UZondi naye wayephakathi kwabo. Phela akazikhohlwa nje unkabi. Amadoda asukuma akhuleka, aphinde ahlala phansi esezimisele ngokulalela inkulumo. Ngaphandle kokuchitha isikhathi, thwasu uMqoqi esukuma. Wamoyizela wabonga lonke ibandla ngokuzidela liphumelele kulembizo, yize amakhaza eshubisa umkantsha. Waphetha ngokuchi: 
"Sengizibonele kahle ukuthi ninenhlonipho ngempela bantu bakithi eNhlangwini. Sekuyophuma nje eceleni labo mina nobaba kanye nani nonke lapha eNhlangwini, esingasoze sababekezelela. Labo asebeze behamba bezincoma emaphephandabeni bezibiza ngo'Makadebona'.

Amandl' Esambane 
Kwashuba umoya. kwathuleka lapho uZondi eseqedile ukuyifunda lendaba kulengosi. Abonakala amadoda ebheka phansi. K wabonakala ukuthi amagama kaMakadebona' ayitholile indawo ezinhliziyweni zamadoda. Kanti labo ab,abehleli ngaphambili. kakhulukazi inkosi noZwelonke kanye noZondl. babonakala bembuka ngelokuhlola insimu uthisha uMzolo. Kodwa yena wabonakala enganake lutho nje. UMqoqi naye wakubona lokho. Washeshe wasukuma wacela uZondi ukuthi aphinde aqhubeke nokufunda ngezansi kwamagama athi; 'Yimina uMakadebona', Nangempela wakwenza lokho. ~Zo?di. Wafunda nje umbhalo omfishane owawuthi: 'Phenya ekhasml leslkhomblsa. ubone isithombe saleliciko elizibiza ngo'Makadebona,' . .Hhayi-ke. wonke amadoda ahlahla amehlo, efisa ukuyibona ephepheni mSlZwa yakwa Mzolo. Ini! Laphenywa iphepha. savela isithombe, Kwavela bani pho! Wo! Ngiyakutshela wena. Kwavela isithombe somfanekiso omkhulu, owawungawusika uwunamathisele odongeni uma uthanda. Kwak~yisiphalaI:~ala senrokazi athi lapho nje eyithi nhla uZondi, hhiya wayazi nJengoba azl mgemuva lesandla sakhe. Wake wathula eyigqolozele. Kwaze kwaqhubeka uMqoqi wathi: "Qhubeka phela bab'uZondi usifundele ukuthi kuthiwa ubani loMakadebona," Kodwa lutho wena bo, Endaweni yalokho, wabonakala enyukubala ebusweni uZondi, lJukuduku, zavele zazehlela nje mi izinyembezi. Wazama ukuqhubeka nokufunda umbhalo lowo owawungezansi kwesithombe. kodwa lutho wasimze wabindeka nje. kalavuma ukuphuma emlonyeni izwi. 
   "Nango-ke eseqala lemikhuba yakhe. Akasafundi ngani?" Kwasho indoda yakwaNdlovu ihlebela eyayiseduze kwayo. 
   Ngisho nalabo awayehleli nabo ngaphambili uZondi. basimze baxakeka nje .. Kwathi ngesikade, wazidela amathambo wafunda. Phela ngezansi kweslphalaphala leso okwabe kungumunru amaziyo. kwakubhalwe kwathiwa: 
"La osesithombeni esingenhla, inkosazane uNobuhle Zulu indodakazi

Umphumela Wokugclna Wothando 
   Nebala walithatha uMqoqi walidlulisela ebandla. Ulithatha nje uselicosha phansi, seliqathakile nakulaba ebebeliphuca uZondi. Nangempela amadoda asibona isithombe ukuthi sifana ncimishi naleso sentokazi abayibona ixhawulana noMqoqi mzukwana kunedili elaliseThekwini. Ngempela ngempela, kwakuyindodakazi kaMbhekeni nezinqotho zayo. 
   Kwathi kusenjalo, njengalokhu phela kwase kuvungazela, walithulisa ibandla uMqoqi wathi: "Hhayi-ke Nhlangwini, impendulo yembizo seniyitholile nonke. Sonke lapha eNhlangwini siyazi ukuthi umuntu okhuluma njengaloMakadebona', sivumelane ngokuthi asimdingi lapha kwelakithi. Uyisihlava esibi. Besilokhu sisola uMzolo, kanti sidlala ngaye. Kube kuhleke sazibonela isithombe salempethu esingayidingi. Ngisho ngoba inkulumo yakhe kwazi wonke umuntu ukuthi, ngisho nenkosi engubaba kanye nani nje nonkana, aniyifuni nalapho ihambe khona. Pho-ke, ngingenzani ngomuntu onenkulumo egxekwa isizwe? Impela ngabe kaningihloniphi. Lilonke-ke nje, kusobala ukuthi ilobolo liya eMbo kwaMkhize. Ngiyabonga." 
   Wathi ewaqeda lawomazwi uMqoqi, yabe inkosi kanye nalabo eyayihleli nabo ngaphambili, sebeyozingenela endlini, kanti ikhehla lakwaMthembu kanye namanye amadoda, baxhawula uthisha uMzolo. Yachitheka imbizo kungasakhulekwanga komkhulu njengasemihleni. 
   Kwathi ngenyanga kaLwezi, kuwona lowo nyaka, hhiya, zawushaya komkhulu. Impelesi kamakoti, kwakuyisiphalaphala sentokazi yakwaDukuza, uNobuhle Zulu. Kanti eyenkosana uMqoqi, kwakuyinsizwa okwathiwa uSikhumbuzo Msomi. Kwaba kuhle kwadela. 
   Kwathi ngemuva konyaka kushadiwe, uMaMkhize intokazi yaseMbo, yabonakala ihleli phansi yenabile, ibele ilikhiphele ngaphandle. Yayidamane iyimbambatha kancane lento eyayiyigodle esifubeni. Phela, yayincelisa futhi ishushuzela indodana yabo benoMqoqi abase beyiphiwe ophezulu. Kwakuyimambane impela, kubonakala ukuthi iyoba inkosi yaseNhlangwini em inyakeni ezayo. Zabanjalo-ke izindaba zezintokazi ezimbili zasebukhosini. 
   Ngisho nanamhlanje, abantu baseNhlangwini uma behlangene bebusa, bayazixoxa izindaba kanye nezigameko esezedl ula. Kodwa basuke bengakazixoxi zonke uma bengakayixoxi indaba kaNobuhle, indodakazi kaMbhekeni, isigwili sakwaDukuza eStanget. Uma sebeyixoxa, wo! Ngiyakutshela wena! Bheka-ke, ubazi nawe abantu baseNhlangwini. Bavele bayisuse phansi baze bayoyikhipha phezulu. Bayixoxa bayixoxe, bese ekugcineni uzwe omunye ebubula ethi: 
"Wo! Hhe! Yekanini 'AMANDL' ESAMBANE', simba umgodi, kanti 
kasizuwulala. "
